<review>Advent Property Management has been managing our San Diego properties since 2008. We live out of the area, (near Pasadena, Ca), and so we needed someone local to take care of our rentals. I spent a long time interviewing different companies because I didn't know anyone in the San Diego area, nor did I have any referrals for anyone there. I eventually chose Advent PM and have not been disappointed. There have been problems with tenants now and then, but that's typical. No matter how good a tenant looks on paper, issues can come up. What matters is how capable the management company is at solving those inevitable issues that arise up...be it tenant or repairs, etc. It's not just about collecting the money every month. Craig and his team have proven themselves more than capable time and time again. Rhonda in the repairs department is fantastic as well! Craig is a great problem solver overall! I'm so happy to have Advent taking care of our properties. I know I don't have to worry about it. His team there is easy to get a hold of. <Gmap_id>0x80c2c0e6bf4a997d:0x6f321c93e90750a<//Gmap_id></record></dataset><record>
<GmapID>0x80c2c0e6bf4a997d:0x6f321c93e90750a<//GmapID>< review>
I decided to try this place on a whim and found it to be good, but no where near the best. The table service here is a welcome touch. Please note that you pay after you have eaten, and they only accept cash. There is an ATM on location, but frankly I would be VERY weary of using it - expensive fees or worse may be waiting in store. The sauce on my cheese enchiladas was excellent, it had a great depth of flavor that was slightly spicy but not overpowering. I thought the amount of cheese was just right, although the overall size of the enchiladas is not too big. The rice on the other hand was a bit of a letdown. There was nothing off-putting about it, but it just tasted sort of bland. The beans were a bit better, but still had my yearning for more flavor. As with all of these small Mexican restaurants the mini salad they add is a nice touch but absolutely nothing to write home about, I noted several large pieces of lettuce that were from the base of the lettuce (that white, hard bit) which were totally inedible. The drink selection here features many glass bottles varieties of Mexican favorites, such as Coca-Cola and Jarritos. Overall it was nothing special, but was good enough to satisfy a hungry individual. I might be inclined at a later date to give El Ruby one more chance to impress me. Also, the menu on the wall is in Spanish, but has pictures to help you decide what you want if Spanish is not your forte.</review>

< text>
I work in Rescue and we need to stretch our $$ to provide the best vet care possible to our dogs. The owner of Warner Ave was gracious to extend to us a rescue discount which the manager Guy initiated. Thank you Guy!!
We were able to have a senior dog in desperate need of a dental taken care of by Dr. Pluskat. Dr. P is very enthusiastic. She called me soon after the dental to let me know how George was doing and how many teeth she had to remove. He also had a tumor which needed to be biopsied, she walked me through the entire procedure and gave me her opinion of the determination of the tumor. She was correct, it was benign. This was my first dog that had had to have so many teeth removed. I was given excellent instructions (written & verbal) on his after care, along with medication to make him more comfortable.

< review>
I would not recommend that anybody bring their animal to this animal clinic.
We brought in our 3 year old kitten for an appointment recently at 9 PM because he was having trouble urinating and was meowing in discomfort.
First impressions were the office was tiny, dirty, and had an odor that did not speak "hospital" to me; the staff seemed disinterested.
Dr. Pluskat was rough-handed on getting our scared kitty out of his carrier and feeling around for his bladder. After a 1 minute evaluation, they gave us a quote for a 1-3 night hospital stay with catheter to drain his bladder and IV for $1500-$2000. We felt we had no choice as no other options were given for home treatment so we agreed and let them take him back.
At around 11:45 PM we received an update call that our kitty was asleep and draining and all sounded okay.
The next morning at 8 AM, we received a phone call from Dr. Black saying that our cat had died overnight.
The explanation we received was that his kidneys possibly failed causing his heart to stop, but we were distraught at the news.
We had no idea he was in a life-threatening situation, or we would have taken him to a 24 hour clinic.
I would not recommend having your animals evaluated here, especially overnight or if you think it's an emergency.
We left hurt and angry not knowing or getting a straight answer if our kitty was actually that sick (he was bright and vibrant leading up to this day), or wondering if the Doctors had accidentally overdosed him on drugs or sedatives and left him in an unstable condition overnight alone with no supervision.
Please consider our story if you're wondering whether to bring your loved ones here, as our joy was taken from our lives under the hands of a very callous staff, with hardly a meaningful "sorry your cat died", and a $1000 bill with three papers all being left of our kitty.<//review>

<user_id>106833195914379298582</user_id><username>Denise Shook< /username><date>1505611734638</date><Rating>4</Rating>< Review>
Really closer to 4.9 stars. This is the sister to beach city animal hospital. This location stays open til midnite sunday thru thursday - in case your fourlegged kids need emergency care. The staff and drs. are very nice and REALLY CARE about our kids. Both beach city and warner ave. Locations give great service, are knowlegable, efficienct, patient with their patients...AND VERY TOLERANT of the parents and any questions you may have. Prices are fair and you get a discount if you pay cash. My kids have been coming to these two locations for 6yrs and i've always gotten excellent service.  Their late nite hours really came in handy, VCA was the only facility that was open 24hrs , but the cost is more than human ER's. Warner avenue started staying open late and were a Godsend for those 'too serious' to wait situations. THANK YOU warner ave. for working late to ensure our kids get the medical attention needed...WHEN ITS NEEDED.</Review>

<Rate>5< /Rate>< Review>
I took this class on the spur-of-the-moment, and I'm glad I did.  The class is a load of fun.  I took the accelerated course, which means I had to pack in the studying, which I suggest doing, because it isn't easy learning 70 some-odd recipes, not to mention the other information that you have to memorize, like the classifications of the liquors, interacting with  guests, and the like.
Also probably worth mentioning is the fact that I, before the class, had next to no knowledge about alcohol.  I wouldn't have known my brandy from my bourbon.  I probably wouldn't have been able to pronounce cognac properly.  After the class, I feel way more informed than I could have ever been, even if I taught myself.  There's a lot of information to pack inside your brain, especially in 40 hours, but the destination is well worth the trip.  Even if you don't plan on getting a bartending job after this class, I'd still recommend taking the class, if only due to the fact that you learn so much.  Alcohol is so prevalent around the world that this won't be information that you never use.

tl;dr; Fun, informative, go, now< /Review>

<userid>107088731787258562988</userid>< Review>
Where do I start...

First of all, before I decided to take this class, I was asking one of my friend who has been bartending for ten years to teach me to barten, and he said " yeah no problem, it's easy, don't go to bartending school...", but the problem is he has been super busy at work and the time that we met, we just play golf and just have fun, so I decided to started searching the bartending school with out telling him.

Lots of school pop up on my computer screen. few schools got some really good reviews and one of them is Socal Bartending. I checked all the detail on every school that I was interest in and went through all pictures and everything until I started got a feeling about this school, then I sent an email about some questions that I had, and It got reply so quickly, so I decided to take this class.

First day of the class, everything looks exactly like I thought. the class is really small which is great, so you can being so close to the trainer and ask anything you want anytime. You also have your own station with your buddy who will help you through this course with so much fun. You also have a book ( school's own book ) that will cover pretty much anything that you need to know about bartender. My favorite part about the book is it short and just go right to the points ! I'm sure is you go buy a book for bartending, you probably ending up reading like 100 pages or more.

After I finished the course, I feel like this school just make everything about bartending look so easy to me. I just ended up automatically knowing 70+ main drinks  without trying so hard to remember it. I also feel much much more confidence about bartending knowledge.The lessons that this school prepare will take you step by step until the end, and you're gonna get the same feeling that I have right now.

Thanks again for everything :)
-Shark</Review>
